The Grand Historian read the Spring and Autumn Annals, calendars, genealogies, and records, reaching King Li of Zhou, never failed to put down the book and sigh. He said: 'Alas, Shi Zhi foresaw it!' Zhou used ivory chopsticks and Jizi sighed. Zhou way declined, poets based it on bed curtains, Guanjun was made. Benevolence and righteousness declined, Lumning satirized it. And when it came to King Li, because he hated hearing his faults criticized, the nobles feared execution and disaster arose, King Li then fled to Zhi, chaos began from the capital, and the Gonghe administered government. After this, some used force to govern, strong oppressed weak, raised armies without requesting the Son of Heaven. Yet holding the righteousness of the royal house, using punitive expeditions as covenant alliance leaders, government was by the five hegemons, feudal lords acted wantonly, extravagant and licentious without propriety, traitorous ministers and usurping sons arose increasingly. Qi, Jin, Qin, Chu in the time of Chengzhou were very insignificant, enfeoffments of either one hundred li or fifty li. Jin blocked the three rivers, Qi leaned on the eastern sea, Chu bordered Jiang and Huai, Qin relied on Yongzhou's fortifications, the four seas rose in succession, alternated as hegemonic lords, those whom Wen and Wu praised and greatly enfeoffed, all awed and submitted. Therefore Confucius clarified the kingly way, visited over seventy rulers, none could employ him, therefore he went west to observe the Zhou house, discussed historical records and old traditions, began from Lu and arranged the Spring and Autumn Annals, above recording Yin, below reaching Ai's capture of the unicorn, condensed its wording, removed its complications, to establish righteous principles, the kingly way was complete, human affairs were thorough. The seventy disciples' followers orally received his transmitted meanings, for there were satirical, critical, praising, taboo, diminishing words that could not be seen in writing. Lu gentleman Zuo Qiuming feared disciples would each go to different doctrines, each comfortable in their own opinions, losing the truth, therefore following Confucius's historical records fully discussed their words, completed the Zuoshi Spring and Autumn Annals. Duo Jiao made the transmission for Chu Wei Wang, for the king could not fully observe the Spring and Autumn Annals, selected successes and failures, in the end forty chapters, became the Duoshi minor work. In Zhao Xiao Cheng Wang's time, his chancellor Yu Qing gathered above from Spring and Autumn, observed below recent trends, also wrote eight scrolls, became the Yu shi Spring and Autumn. LÃ¼ Buwei, Qin Zhuang Xiang Wang's chancellor, also observed above ancient veneration, selected and gathered Spring and Autumn, collected six states' affairs, made eight views, six discussions, twelve records, became the LÃ¼ shi Spring and Autumn. And like Xun Qing, Mengzi, Gongsun Gu, Han Fei and others, each often gathered Spring and Autumn's text to write books, different ways of counting. Han chancellor Zhang Cang calendared the five virtues, upper grand master Dong Zhongshu pushed Spring and Autumn meanings, considerably wrote texts.

Twelfth year, twenty-second year, fourteenth year, seventeenth year

478 Forty-second year, seventeenth year, third year, thirty-fourth year, thirteenth year, eleventh year, thirty-ninth year, third year, Zhuang Gong insulted Rong Zhou people, Rong Zhou people allied with Zhao Jian Zi attacked Zhuang Gong, fled out. Thirteenth year, twenty-third year, fifteenth year, eighteenth year, Yue defeated us.

477 Jiazi forty-third year, Jing Wang died. Eighteenth year, twenty-seventh year died. Fourth year, twenty-fifth year died. Thirty-fifth year, thirty-seventh year died. Fourteenth year died, son Li Gong Gong established. Twelfth year, fifty-seventh year died. Forty-sixth year, fourteenth year died. Wei Jun Qi first year, Shi Fu drove Qi out, Che again entered. Fourteenth year, nineteenth year died, twenty-fourth year, thirty-eighth year died. Sixteenth year, twenty-eighth year died. Nineteenth year, twenty-third year died.

The Grand Historian says: Confucian scholars cut their meanings, dashing speakers gallop their words, not strive to comprehensively their beginnings and ends; Calendar people take their years and months, several families exalt divine fate, genealogies and records only record posthumous names, their words brief, wish one view the essentials difficult. Therefore tabulated twelve feudal lords, from Gonghe to Confucius, table shows Spring and Autumn Annals, Guo Yu scholars criticize flourishing decline great pointers seen in the scroll, for completing learning governing ancient texts essential summary.
